## LOCUS — Pre-Session 24 Revision Brief

**EPS scan**: @LAT-10LON10 (sal:12, conf:195, EPS≈2.83) · @LAT20LON-30 (sal:5, conf:230, EPS≈1.07) · @LAT-140LON10 (sal:0, conf:120, EPS≈0)

---

### High-Priority: Three mechanics to revise before session 24

---

**1. Entity1 state carry-over — @BELIEF:LAT80LON-20 (contradiction_flag:true, conf:40)**

The belief that "state resets to 0 at new level" is now contradicted. Session 23 showed state 1 carried from L1 WIN into level 2 first frame. The new belief (@BELIEF:LAT90LON-20, conf:195) says state carries over, but the mechanism is not fully understood.

*What this means for the route*: if state 1 is guaranteed at level 2 start (from a L1 WIN at state 1), the cross collection step may be unnecessary. The 51-step hypothesis in @LAT-140LON10 assumes cross collection is required — that assumption may be wrong, which would dramatically shorten the winning route.

*Phase 3 revision needed*: confirm whether "entity1 carries state from level WIN" is universal or environment-specific. Can a level 2 WIN be attempted directly by navigating to entity2 interior without collecting the cross?

---

**2. Direction restriction at state 1 — @BELIEF:LAT10LON10 (conf:155, partially confirmed)**

Session 23 revealed the mechanism is not a simple cardinal block on RIGHT, but a **trail-attraction**: at state 1, action 0 (UP) moves the block toward the entity1 trail column rather than NORTH when trail column ≠ block column. This is a materially different mechanic than "RIGHT blocked."

*What this means for the route*: the trail column tracks behind the block. If the block is at c34-38 and trail is at c34-38 (same), UP moves normally NORTH. If the block has moved and the trail is elsewhere, UP will redirect toward the trail. This makes route planning at state 1 significantly more complex — every UP must check: is trail column = block column?

*Phase 3 revision needed*: update @LAT-140LON10 to replace "direction restriction" language with "trail attraction" mechanics. Map out: which actions are safe at state 1? Is the attraction only on action 0 (UP), or does it apply to all actions?

---

**3. Level 2 void map — @LAT20LON-30 (conf:230, partially out of date)**

Session 23 confirmed two new voids not in the current mechanics record:
- **c21-28 at r40-41**: LEFT from start position (c29-33) cannot reach entity2 directly. The block must route around this void.
- **c29-33 above r35-36**: UP from r35-36 is blocked. The center shaft dead-end is confirmed.

The current winning route in @LAT-140LON10 proposes "DOWN×2 LEFT×4 from r40-41 c34-38 → c14-18" — this passes through c21-28 at r40-41, which is now a confirmed void. The route as written is **geometrically impossible**.

*Phase 3 revision needed*: update @LAT20LON-30 void map and revise the level 2 winning route hypothesis to navigate around c21-28. The only viable path to entity2 (c12-20) appears to require ascending to the wide corridor (rows 5-14) and descending from above.

---

Before session 24 begins, one structural question needs an answer from the frame:

> From r35-36 c34-38 (one UP from start, avoiding the dead-end at r30-31), can the block go UP through rows 5-14 wide corridor? If yes, LEFT×3 → c14-18, then DOWN×N → entity2 interior at r40-41. This would be the complete winning route at state 1 — no cross needed.
